# HEY THERE. 
# THIS WAS AN IDEA THAT'S BEEN RUNNING IN MY HEAD FOR A BIT, SO I FINALLY DECIDED TO MAKE SOMETHING WITH IT.
# 
# MANY TIMES I'VE HAD PEOPLE ASKING ME IF THEY COULD BORROW SKINS I'VE MADE FOR THEIR OWN PROJECTS, AND IN MOST
# CASES MY ANSWER WAS NO BECAUSE EVERY CUSTOM SKIN I'VE MADE WAS SPECIFICALLY WRITTEN FOR A PARTICULAR WEAPON,
# IT WAS THOUGHT AND DEVELOPED FOR A SPECIFIC REASON, AND IT'D FEEL "WRONG" TO HAVE IT ON ANYTHING OTHER THAN THE
# GUN IT WAS MEANT FOR.
#
# SO, I DECIDED TO MAKE THIS:
# FOLLOWING HERE YOU'LL FIND A BUNCH OF WEAPON SKINS YOU ARE FREE TO USE AS-IS OR MODIFY FREELY FOR YOUR OWN PROJECTS.
# I SPENT A FEW DAYS MAKING A BUNCH OF SKINS I THOUGHT WERE COOL AND ENDED UP WITH ABOUT 60 OF THEM. I HOPE YOU'LL FIND SOMEHTING YOU ENJOY.
# 
# SKINS ARE DIVIDED IN THEMES: I DECIDED TO PICK A FEW MANUFACTURERS AND MAKE SETS OF SKINS THAT WOULD FIT THEM.
# EVERY SKIN IS NAMED INDIVIDUALLY SO YOU CAN FIND IT AND LOOK AT IT IN THE HUGE PREVIEW PICTURE .  . . . . . . . . . . . . . . >>> LINK TO PREVIEW PICTURE (CLICK TO ZOOM!): https://sta.sh/024vmc04blmm
# AT THE VERY END OF THIS FILE YOU'LL ALSO FIND A BUNCH OF SKINS THAT ARE JUST SIMPLE SOLID COLORS IN CASE YOU PREFER 
# SOMETHING CLEAN, QUICK AND EASY TO JUST COPY/PASTE AND DON'T FEEL LIKE HAVING ANYTHING MORE ELABORATED.
#
# IMPORTANT NOTE: EVERY SKIN IN THIS FILE IS FORMATTED TO A SPECIFIC WEAPON, HOWEVER MOST WILL WORK ON MANY OTHER WEAPONS AS WELL.
# ALL YOU NEED TO DO IS COPY/PASTE THE SKIN AND MAKE SURE YOUR MAPPING IS CORRECT. IF YOU'RE NOT SURE HOW TO, LOOK UP MAPPING ON MY SKIN GUIDE.
# BECAUSE OF HOW DIFFERENT GUNS CAN READ DIFFERENT PATTERNS AND DECALS, A FEW OF THESE SKINS MIGHT NOT BE PASTED ON EVERY SINGLE WEAPON.
#
# IF YOU HAVE ADDITIONAL QUESTIONS FEEL FREE TO ASK!
#
# THANK YOU, AND I HOPE YOU'LL FIND SOMETHING YOU LIKE :)
